Type Chart Summary:
Normal: Super effective against None. Not very effective against Rock, Steel. No effect on Ghost.
Fire: Super effective against Grass, Ice, Bug, Steel. Not very effective against Fire, Water, Rock, Dragon. No effect on None.
Water: Super effective against Fire, Ground, Rock. Not very effective against Water, Grass, Dragon. No effect on None.
Grass: Super effective against Water, Ground, Rock. Not very effective against Fire, Grass, Poison, Flying, Bug, Dragon, Steel. No effect on None.
Electric: Super effective against Water, Flying. Not very effective against Grass, Electric, Dragon. No effect on Ground.
Ice: Super effective against Grass, Ground, Flying, Dragon. Not very effective against Fire, Water, Ice, Steel. No effect on None.
Fighting: Super effective against Normal, Ice, Rock, Dark, Steel. Not very effective against Poison, Flying, Psychic, Bug, Fairy. No effect on Ghost.
Poison: Super effective against Grass, Fairy. Not very effective against Poison, Ground, Rock, Ghost. No effect on Steel.
Ground: Super effective against Fire, Electric, Poison, Rock, Steel. Not very effective against Grass, Bug. No effect on Flying.
Flying: Super effective against Grass, Fighting, Bug. Not very effective against Electric, Rock, Steel. No effect on None.
Psychic: Super effective against Fighting, Poison. Not very effective against Psychic, Steel. No effect on Dark.
Bug: Super effective against Grass, Psychic, Dark. Not very effective against Fire, Fighting, Poison, Flying, Ghost, Steel, Fairy. No effect on None.
Rock: Super effective against Fire, Ice, Flying, Bug. Not very effective against Fighting, Ground, Steel. No effect on None.
Ghost: Super effective against Psychic, Ghost. Not very effective against Dark. No effect on Normal.
Dragon: Super effective against Dragon. Not very effective against Steel. No effect on Fairy.
Dark: Super effective against Psychic, Ghost. Not very effective against Fighting, Dark, Fairy. No effect on None.
Steel: Super effective against Ice, Rock, Fairy. Not very effective against Fire, Water, Electric, Steel. No effect on None.
Fairy: Super effective against Fighting, Dragon, Dark. Not very effective against Fire, Poison, Steel. No effect on None.

Abomasnow is a Grass/Ice-type Pokémon. Weak to: Fire (4x), Fighting, Poison, Flying, Bug, Rock, Steel. Resists: Water, Grass, Electric, Ground. Immune to: None. Evolution: It evolves from Snover starting at level 40. Locations: X: Route 17; Y: Route 17; Omega Ruby: Trade from X & Y; Alpha Sapphire: Trade from X & Y; Sun: Trade from Ultra Sun/Ultra Moon; Moon: Trade from Ultra Sun/Ultra Moon; Ultra Sun: Ultra Space Wilds; Ultra Moon: Ultra Space Wilds; Sword: Route 10 , Axew's Eye , Dusty Bowl , Giant's Mirror , Giant's Seat , Hammerlocke Hills , Lake of Outrage , Max Raid Battles: Dusty Bowl , Giant's Cap , Hammerlocke Hills; Shield: Route 10 , Axew's Eye , Dusty Bowl , Giant's Mirror , Giant's Seat , Hammerlocke Hills , Lake of Outrage , Max Raid Battles: Dusty Bowl , Giant's Cap , Hammerlocke Hills; Brilliant Diamond: Mt. Coronet; Shining Pearl: Mt. Coronet; Legends: Arceus: Alabaster Icelands : Avalugg's Legacy , Glacier Terrace or nearby , Coronet Highlands : Massive Mass Outbreak , Alabaster Icelands : Massive Mass Outbreak. Stats: HP 90/Atk 132/Def 105/SpA 132/SpD 105/Spe 30.
Abra is a Psychic-type Pokémon. Weak to: Bug, Ghost, Dark. Resists: Fighting, Psychic. Immune to: None. Evolution: It evolves into Kadabra starting at level 16, which evolves into Alakazam when traded, or when exposed to a Linking Cord (Pokémon Legends: Arceus). Stats: HP 25/Atk 20/Def 15/SpA 105/SpD 55/Spe 90.
Absol is a Dark-type Pokémon. Weak to: Fighting, Bug, Fairy. Resists: Ghost, Dark. Immune to: Psychic. Evolution: While it is not known to evolve into or from any other Pokémon, Absol can Mega Evolve into Mega Absol using the Absolite. Evolution: It evolves from Shelmet when traded for a Karrablast, a Pokémon that evolves into Escavalier simultaneously. Neither evolves if at least one holds an Everstone during the trade. Aerodactyl is a Rock/Flying-type Pokémon. Weak to: Water, Electric, Ice, Rock, Steel. Resists: Normal, Fire, Poison, Flying, Bug. Immune to: Ground. Alcremie is a Fairy-type Pokémon. Weak to: Poison, Steel. Resists: Fighting, Bug, Dark. Immune to: Dragon. Evolution: It evolves from Milcery while holding a Sweet when its Trainer spins and strikes a pose. The form it takes upon evolving depends on the time of the day, the length of the spin, and whether the Trainer was spinning clockwise or counterclockwise. Its appearance is further determined by the type of Sweet that is held. Locations: X: Not found in this generation; Y: Not found in this generation; Omega Ruby: Not found in this generation; Alpha Sapphire: Not found in this generation; Sun: Not found in this generation; Moon: Not found in this generation; Ultra Sun: Not found in this generation; Ultra Moon: Not found in this generation; Sword: Max Raid Battles: Bridge Field , Lake of Outrage , Gigantamax Raid Battles: Bridge Field; Shield: Max Raid Battles: Bridge Field , Lake of Outrage , Gigantamax Raid Battles: Bridge Field; Brilliant Diamond: Not found in Brilliant Diamond; Shining Pearl: Not found in Shining Pearl; Legends: Arceus: Not found in Legends Arceus. Stats: HP 65/Atk 60/Def 75/SpA 110/SpD 121/Spe 64.

Furfrou is a Normal-type Pokémon. Weak to: Fighting. Resists: None. Immune to: Ghost. Evolution: While it is not known to evolve into or from any other Pokémon, Furfrou can have its hair trimmed into nine different styles to change its appearance. The styles include the Star, Diamond, Heart, Pharaoh, Kabuki, La Reine, Matron, Dandy, and Debutante Trim. A trimmed Furfrou will revert into its Natural Form if five days have passed since it was trimmed without being deposited in the PC, or if it is deposited in (Generation VI) or withdrawn from (Generation VII) the PC. Magearna is a Steel/Fairy-type Pokémon. Weak to: Fire, Ground. Resists: Normal, Grass, Ice, Flying, Psychic, Bug (0.25x), Rock, Dark, Fairy. Immune to: Poison, Dragon. Evolution: While it is not known to evolve into or from any other Pokémon, Magearna has a second form colored gold and red, known as Original Color Magearna that, while present in Pokémon Sun, Moon, Ultra Sun, and Ultra Moon, was not made available until the release of Generation VIII's Pokémon HOME. Manaphy is a Water-type Pokémon. Weak to: Grass, Electric. Resists: Fire, Water, Ice, Steel. Immune to: None. Evolution: It is not known to evolve into or from any other Pokémon, but it has the unusual ability to breed, despite being a Mythical Pokémon. It is also unusual in that its offspring are Phione, which do not evolve into Manaphy, and that Manaphy Eggs have a different appearance from other Pokémon Eggs. Rayquaza is a Dragon/Flying-type Pokémon. Weak to: Ice (4x), Rock, Dragon, Fairy. Resists: Fire, Water, Grass (0.25x), Fighting, Bug. Immune to: Ground. Evolution: While it is not known to evolve into or from any other Pokémon, Rayquaza can Mega Evolve into Mega Rayquaza if it knows Dragon Ascent, but only if it is not holding a Z-Crystal. In Pokémon Omega Ruby and Alpha Sapphire, the Rayquaza featured in the Delta Episode must be caught (which requires it to eat the Meteorite) before the player can Mega Evolve any Rayquaza. Shaymin is a Grass-type Pokémon. Weak to: Fire, Ice, Poison, Flying, Bug. Resists: Water, Grass, Electric, Ground. Immune to: None. Evolution: While it is not known to evolve into or from another Pokémon, Shaymin has a second Forme activated by using a Gracidea flower in the daytime. Its original Forme, Land Forme, will then become the Grass/Flying-type Sky Forme. Shaymin's Sky Forme will revert into and remain in its Land Forme during the night or when frozen. Other circumstances may also cause it to revert. Stats: Unknown.

Unown is a Psychic-type Pokémon. Weak to: Bug, Ghost, Dark. Resists: Fighting, Psychic. Immune to: None. Evolution: While it is not known to evolve into or from any other Pokémon, as of Generation III, Unown has 28 derivative shapes, chronicled in the Unown Mode in Generation II and the Unown Report in HeartGold and SoulSilver. There are 26 Latin alphabet characters, plus ? (question mark) and ! (exclamation mark) introduced in Generation III. In Generation II, its shape is determined by its individual values; in Generation III, it is determined by its personality value; from Generation IV onward, it is determined by a separate form identifier. Wurmple is a Bug-type Pokémon. Weak to: Fire, Flying, Rock. Resists: Grass, Fighting, Ground. Immune to: None. Evolution: Wurmple will evolve into either Silcoon or Cascoon starting at level 7 depending on its personality value. As personality values cannot be influenced or seen by the player, what a given Wurmple will evolve into is essentially random. From there, the Silcoon or Cascoon will evolve again starting at level 10 into Beautifly or Dustox respectively.
